PART III - LANDS  
 
Title Registration 
 
REGISTRATION  OF  TITLE ACT, No.  21 OF  1998  
 
Declaration  of  Determination  of  the  Commissioner  of  Title  Settlement  under  Section  14 
 
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 14 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I, the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 4 and 155 of Block 01, 
contained in the Cadastral Map No. 510600 , situated in the Village of Kalalpitiya, within the Grama Niladhari Division of No. 343 - 
Kalalpitiya in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla, in the District of Gampaha, in the Province of Western, referred to in 
Notice No. 51/0365 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 1738/22 of 29th December, 2011 in 
terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998. 
 
 
 K.A.K. R
ANJITH  DHARMAPALA , 
 Commissioner of Title Settlement. 
 
Land Title Settlement Department, 
No. 1200/6, â€œMihikatha Meduraâ€, 
Rajamalwatta Road, 
Battaramulla. 
18th August, 2016.

REGISTRATION  OF  TITLE ACT, No.  21 OF  1998  
 
Declaration  of  Determination  of  the  Commissioner  of  Title  Settlement  under  Section  14 
 
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 14 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I, the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 151, 152, 153, 164, 193, 
198, 216 and 235 of Block 01, contained in the Cadastral Map No. 510618, situated in the Village of Webadagalla, within the Grama 
Niladhari Division of No. 349 - Maduwegedara in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla, in the District of Gampaha, in the 
Province of Western, referred to in Notice No. 51/0845 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 
1959/15 of 24th March, 2016 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998. 
 
 
 K.A.K. R

Niladhari Division of No. 349 - Maduwegedara in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla, in the District of Gampaha, in the 
Province of Western, referred to in Notice No. 51/0826 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 
1948/29  of 06th January, 2016 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.

REGISTRATION  OF  TITLE ACT, No.  21 OF  1998  
 
Declaration  of  Determination  of  the  Commissioner  of  Title  Settlement  under  Section  14 
 
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 14 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I, the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 569 and 570 of Block 01, 
contained in the Cadastral Map No. 510641, situated in the Village of Pinnagolla, within the Grama Niladhari Division of No. 348I - 
Pinnagolla in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla, in the District of Gampaha, in the Province of Western, referred to in 
Notice No. 51/0472 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 1776/33 of 20th September, 2012 in 
terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998. 
 
 
 K.A.K. R

clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 44, 45, 47, 54, 85, 90, 91,

District of Gampaha, in the Province of Western, referred to in Notice No. 51/0724 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly 
published in the Gazette  No. 1895/35 of 02nd January, 2015 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.
